Therefore, Yin Jaundice is often warmed with hot broth, or a cloth soaked in broth is applied to the chest and abdomen, or hot broth is held in a ladle and placed under the navel for fomentation.[50p]

    其病愈者，曾治赵显宗病伤寒至六七日，因服下药太过致发黄，其脉沉细迟无力，皮肤凉，发躁欲于泥中卧，喘呕，小便赤濇，先投茵陈橘皮汤，喘呕止；次服小茵陈汤半剂，脉微出，不欲于泥中卧；次日又服茵陈附子汤半剂，四肢发热，小便二三升，当日中大汗而愈。似此治愈者，不一一录。凡伤寒病黄，每遇太阳或太阴司天岁，若下之太过，往往变成阴黄。盖辰戌太阳寒水司天，水来犯土，丑未太阴湿土司天，土气不足，即脾胃虚弱，亦水来侵犯，多变此证也。　　伤寒发黄黄疸等证，多由湿热。如小水不利，或黄或赤，或小腹胀满不痛，或大便实而渴甚，脉来沉实有力，皆湿热之证，轻则茵陈五苓散，重则茵陈汤，分利小便，清血泻火，则黄自退矣。然黄有阴证，及诸治法，俱详于前，宜参用之。[51p]

    Those who recover from this illness often have been treated for Zhao Xianzong’s cold damage lasting six or seven days. Due to excessive medication, they develop jaundice. Their pulse is deep, thin, slow, and weak, their skin is cool, their hair is frizzy, they desire to lie in mud, they experience wheezing and vomiting, and their urine is red and clouded. Initially, I prescribed a decoction of artemisia and dried orange peel, which alleviated the wheezing and vomiting; then, half a dose of the small artemisia decoction was given, and their pulse slightly improved, reducing the desire to lie in mud. The next day, half a dose of the artemisia and aconite decoction was administered, their limbs became warm, they urinated two to three liters, and they sweated profusely on that day, resulting in recovery. Cases like this are too numerous to list individually.

    In cases of cold damage with jaundice, it is often associated with the celestial bodies of the sun or the moon. If purged excessively, it often turns to a severe jaundice. The presence of the Chen and Xu (the hours of the day associated with the sun) indicates cold water in charge, which invades the earth; for the Chou and Wei (the hours associated with the moon), damp earth is in charge, leading to insufficient earth energy, resulting in spleen and stomach weakness. This allows water to invade, frequently resulting in this condition.

    Jaundice from cold damage often arises from damp heat. Symptoms may include difficulty with small urination, either yellow or red urine, a distended but painless lower abdomen, or firm stools with extreme thirst. The pulse is deep, solid, and strong, indicating damp heat. For mild cases, a formula of artemisia and five grain dispersal may be sufficient; for severe cases, the artemisia decoction can be used to promote urination, clear the blood, and eliminate heat, thus causing the jaundice to recede. However, there are also cases of yin jaundice with different treatment methods; these are detailed above and should be referred to accordingly.[51p]

    　　　　石室秘箓 【清　陈士铎】

    　　　　　黄疸

    　　黄疸之证，一身尽黄，两目亦黄，却是死证。倘初起即治之，亦未必即死也。我有奇方，名为消黄去瘅汤。茵陈三钱，薏仁、车前子各三两，茯苓二两，肉桂三分，水煎服。一连四剂，黄去瘅消矣。黄疸虽成于湿热，毕竟脾虚不能分消水湿，以致郁而成黄。吾用茯苓、薏仁、车前大剂为君，分消水湿，仍是健脾固气之药；少用茵陈以解湿热，用肉桂引入膀胱，尽从小便而出，无事张皇，而暗解其湿热之横。此方之淡而妙，简而神也。四剂之后减半，加白朮一两，煎汤饮之。再用四剂，则全愈而无后患矣。　　黄疸之证，原不宜死。[52p]

    Secret Prescriptions of the Stone Chamber
    By Chen Shiduo of the Qing Dynasty

    On Jaundice

    The symptoms of jaundice include yellowing of the entire body and eyes, which indicates a death sentence. However, if treated at the onset, it may not necessarily lead to death. I possess a remarkable formula called the Decoction to Eliminate Jaundice and Resolve Dampness. It consists of three qian of Artemisia, three liang each of Job's tears and Plantago seeds, two liang of Poria, and three fen of cinnamon, which is to be boiled and consumed. After four doses, the jaundice will disappear and the dampness will resolve.

    Although jaundice arises from damp heat, the root cause is ultimately a deficiency of the spleen that fails to regulate and eliminate water and dampness, resulting in stagnation and jaundice. I prescribe large doses of Poria, Job's tears, and Plantago as the chief ingredients to dispel water dampness while also being fortifying for the spleen and qi; a small amount of Artemisia is used to resolve damp heat, and the cinnamon is included to guide it to the bladder for elimination through urination, subtly addressing the damp heat in the process. This formula is both light and exquisite, simple yet miraculous.

    After the first four doses, reduce the amount by half and add one liang of Atractylodes, then brew and drink. Use another four doses, and they will recover completely without subsequent issues. The symptoms of jaundice should generally not lead to death.[52p]

    然治之不得法，往往生变为死。盖黄疸外感之湿易治，内伤之湿难医。外感单治湿而疸随愈，内伤单治湿而疸难痊。泻水则气愈消，发汗则精愈泄。又何能黄疸之速愈哉？我有方，单治内伤而得黄疸者，名治内消疸汤。白朮、茯苓、薏仁各一两，茵陈、炒栀子各二钱，陈皮五分，水煎服。此方妙在用白朮、茯苓、薏仁之多，使健脾又复利水，助茵陈、栀子以消湿热，尽从膀胱内消，不必又去退皮肤之湿而皮肤之湿自消。大约此方用之十剂，无不消者，不必十剂之外。服十剂减半，去栀子，再服五剂则全愈，人亦健旺矣。至妙至神之方，有益无损，可为治内伤而感湿者之法。
    　　　　方

    　　猪膏发煎 【仲景，下同】 　治诸黄。　　猪膏半斤　乱发如鸡子大，三枚[53p]

    If treatment methods are not correct, it often transforms life into death. Indeed, jaundice caused by external dampness is easily treated, while those from internal injury are difficult to heal. In cases of external dampness, simply treating the dampness can lead to the recovery from jaundice, whereas treating internal injury solely for dampness makes recovery from jaundice challenging. Purging water diminishes vital energy, and inducing sweat causes loss of essence. How can one expect a rapid recovery from jaundice?

    I have a remedy that treats internal injury causing jaundice, called the Internal Dissipation Jaundice Decoction. It consists of one tael each of Atractylodes macrocephala, Poria, and Job’s tears, two qian each of Artemisia capillaris and fried Gardenia fruit, and five fen of dried tangerine peel, all boiled in water for consumption. The brilliance of this prescription lies in the abundant use of Atractylodes macrocephala, Poria, and Job’s tears, which strengthen the spleen and facilitate water metabolism, assisting Artemisia capillaris and Gardenia fruit in dissipating dampness and heat, all from within the bladder, without the need to additionally expel the dampness from the skin, which will resolve itself. Generally, using this formula for ten doses will result in complete dissipation; it is not necessary to exceed ten doses. After ten doses, reduce to half, eliminate the Gardenia fruit, and take five more doses for full recovery; the person will be strong and vigorous. This is a remarkably effective and miraculous remedy, beneficial and harmless, suitable for treating those with internal injury compounded by dampness.

    Formula:

    Pig fat decoction—treatment for various jaundice. Use half a pound of pig fat, cut into pieces the size of a chicken egg, three pieces.[53p]

    　　右二味，和膏中煎之，发消药成，分再服，病从小便出。
    　　小建中汤　治黄疸，小便自利。
    　　桂枝去皮　甘草炙　生姜各三两　芍药六两　大枣十二枚　胶饴一升　　右六味，以水七升，煮取三升，去滓内胶饴，更上微火消解，温服一升，日三服。
    　　小半夏汤　治黄疸喘满而秽。
    　　半夏一升　生姜半斤
    　　右二味，以水七升，煮取一升半，分温再服。
    　　小柴胡汤　治黄疸，诸劳复而呕者。　　柴胡半斤　黄芩　人参　甘草　生姜各三两　半夏半斤　大枣十二枚　　右七味，以水一斗二升，煮取六升，去滓再煎，取三升，温服一升，日三服。
    　　越婢加朮汤　治里水，一身面目黄肿者。　　麻黄六两　石膏半斤　白朮四两　生姜三两　甘草二两　大枣十五枚　　右六味，以水六升，先煮麻黄，去上沫，内诸药，煮取三升，分温三服。恶风，加附子一枚炮。[54p]

    The two ingredients on the right, harmonized in the decoction, release the medicinal properties; divide and take again, the illness will exit through urination.

    Xiao Jian Zhong Decoction treats jaundice, promoting urination.
    Three taels each of peeled cinnamon twig, honey-fried liquorice, and fresh ginger; six taels of peony root; twelve jujubes; one sheng of glucose syrup. Prepare by boiling with seven sheng of water until three sheng remain; remove the residue and dissolve the glucose syrup over a gentle heat. Take one sheng warm, three times daily.

    Xiao Ban Xia Decoction treats jaundice with wheezing and fullness.
    One sheng of pinellia; half a jin of fresh ginger.
    With these two ingredients, boil with seven sheng of water until one and a half sheng remain; divide and take warm again.

    Xiao Chai Hu Decoction treats jaundice with recurring fatigue and vomiting.
    Half a jin of chih-hao; three taels each of yellow qin, ginseng, licorice, and fresh ginger; half a jin of pinellia; twelve jujubes.
    With these seven ingredients, boil with twelve sheng of water until six sheng remain; remove the residue, re-boil to obtain three sheng; take one sheng warm, three times daily.

    Yue Bi Jia Zhu Decoction treats internal water retention with yellow swelling of the entire body and face.
    Six taels of ephedra; half a jin of gypsum; four taels of atractylodes; three taels of fresh ginger; two taels of licorice; fifteen jujubes.
    With these six ingredients, first boil the ephedra, skimming off the froth; then add the other ingredients and boil until three sheng remain; divide and take warm three times. For aversion to wind, add one processed aconite.[54p]

    　　抵当汤　治黄疸，属血证者。
    　　桃仁二十个，去皮尖　大黄三两，酒浸　水蛭熬　蝱虫各三十个，熬去翅足　　右四味为末，水五升，煮取三升，去滓，温服一升，不可再服。
    　　麻黄连翘赤小豆汤　治黄疸瘀热在里者。　　麻黄去节　连翘根　生姜切，各二两　赤小豆　生梓白皮各一升　甘草炙，一两　大枣十二枚　杏仁四十个，去皮尖　　已上八味，以潦水一斗，先煮麻黄，再沸，去上沫，内诸药，煮取三升，分温三服半。
    　　麻黄汤　治阳明中风，黄疸，脉浮无余证者。　　麻黄去节，三两　桂枝去皮，二两　甘草炙，一两　杏仁汤泡去皮尖，七十个　　右四味，以水九升，先煮麻黄，减二升，去上沫，内诸药，煮取二升半，去滓温服八合，覆取微汗，不须啜粥。余如桂枝汤法。[55p]

    Dìdàng Táng - Treats jaundice associated with blood conditions.
    Twenty peach kernels, skin removed; three liang of rhubarb, soaked in wine; thirty water leeches, boiled; thirty pill millipedes, wings and legs removed. Grind the four ingredients into powder, add five sheng of water, boil down to three sheng, strain out the dregs, and take one sheng warm, not to be repeated.

    Máhuáng Liánqiáo Zhì Xiǎodòu Táng - Treats jaundice with stagnant heat inside.
    Three liang of horse radish (Ephedra), cut off the joints; two liang of honeysuckle roots; two liang of fresh ginger, sliced; one sheng of red beans; one sheng of fresh mulberry bark; one liang of roasted licorice; twelve jujubes; forty peach kernels, skin removed.
    Prepare the first eight ingredients with ten dou of water, first boil the horse radish, remove the foam, add the other medicines, boil to obtain three sheng, divide into three warm doses.

    Máhuáng Táng - Treats Yangming stroke, jaundice, and pulse that floats without residual signs.
    Three liang of horse radish (Ephedra), cut off the joints; two liang of cinnamon twig (Guiling), bark removed; one liang of roasted licorice; seventy peach kernels, soaked in apricot soup and skin removed.
    Prepare the four ingredients with nine sheng of water, first boil the horse radish, reduce to two sheng, remove the foam, add the other medicines, boil down to two and a half sheng, strain and take warm eight he, cover to induce slight sweating, no need to sip porridge. Other procedures follow the method of ginger twig soup.[55p]

    　　五苓散　治黄疸，小便不利。
    　　泽泻一两一分　猪苓去黑　白茯苓去皮　白朮各三分　桂枝去皮，半两　　右捣筛为散拌和，每服抄三钱，白汤调下。去桂名四苓散。
    　　大黄硝石汤　治表和里实疸病。
    　　大黄　黄蘗　硝石各四两，一作滑石　栀子十五枚　　右四味，以水六升，煮取二升，去滓，内硝石，更煮取一升，顿服。
    　　大陷胸汤　治结胸发黄者。
    　　大黄　芒硝各三钱　甘遂末三字匕
    　　右銼如麻豆大，一剂分作二服，每服用水一盏，煮大黄至六分，内硝，煎一二沸，绞汁一字匕半，温服。未快利再服。恶热不利者，以意加服。
    　　茵陈蒿汤 【仲景】 　治寒热不食，食即头眩，心膈不安，久久发黄，名为谷疸。　　茵陈蒿六两　栀子十四枚　大黄二两　　右三味，以水一斗，先煮茵陈，减六升，内三味，煮取三升，去滓，分温三服。小便当利，尿如皂角汁状，色正赤，一宿腹减，黄从小便去也。[56p]

    Wuling Powder is used to treat jaundice and difficulty in urination.
    Ingredients:

    • 1.1 ounces of Zexie
    • Remove the black from Zhuling
    • 0.3 ounces of Bai Fuling (peeled)
    • 0.3 ounces of Baizhu
    • 0.5 ounces of Gui Zhi (peeled)
      Crush and sieve the ingredients, mix well. For each dose, take 0.3 ounces and dissolve in warm water. If Gui Zhi is omitted, it is called Siling Powder.

    Dahuang Xiaoshi Decoction treats exterior and interior excess jaundice.
    Ingredients:

    • 4 ounces of Dahuang
    • 4 ounces of Huangbo
    • 4 ounces of Xiaoshi (some suggest Tofu)
    • 15 pieces of Zhizi
      Boil these four ingredients with 6 liters of water to reduce to 2 liters. Strain, add Xiaoshi, and boil again to yield 1 liter. Take all at once.

    Daxianxiong Decoction is for treating yellowing due to a firm breast mass.
    Ingredients:

    • 0.3 ounces of Dahuang
    • 0.3 ounces of Mangxiao
    • 1 spoon of powdered Gansui
      Grind to a size comparable to a mung bean. Divide into two doses. For each dose, use one cup of water to boil Dahuang down to 60%, add Mangxiao, and simmer one to two times. Strain half a spoon of juice and take warm. If not effective, repeat. Add extra if there is heat and discomfort.

    Yinchenhao Decoction treats chills and fevers, poor appetite, dizziness upon eating, a feeling of unease in the heart, and prolonged yellowing, termed "grain jaundice."
    Ingredients:

    • 6 ounces of Yinchenhao
    • 14 pieces of Zhizi
    • 2 ounces of Dahuang
      Boil these three ingredients with 10 liters of water, first boiling the Yinchenhao to reduce to 6 liters. Then add the other two and boil down to 3 liters. Strain and divide into three warm doses. Urination should increase, resembling dark bean juice in color. After a night's rest, the abdominal swelling should decrease, with yellowing eliminated through urination.[56p]

    　　大建中汤　治胸中大寒，不能饮食，腹中寒气上冲，上下疼痛，不可触近，并阴黄等证。　　人参二两　蜀椒二合，炒去汗　干姜四两　　右三味，以水四升，煮取二升，共滓，内胶饴一升，微火煎取一升半，分二次温服。如一炊顷，可食温粥覆之。
    　　芪芍桂苦酒汤　治黄汗，汗出沾衣如黄蘗汁。　　黄芪五两　白芍药　桂枝各三两
    　　右三味，以苦酒一升，水七升相和，煮取三升，温服一升，当心烦，服至六七日乃解。若心烦不止者，以苦酒阻故也。
    　　桂枝加黄芪汤　治黄疸脉浮而腹中和者，宜汗之。若腹满欲呕吐，懊憹而不和者，宜吐之，不宜汗。　　桂枝　白芍药　生姜各三两　大枣十二枚　黄芪　甘草各二两　　右六味，以水八升，煮取三升，温服一升，须臾饮热稀粥一升余，以助药力，取微汗。若不汗，更服。[57p]

    Great Jianzhong Decoction: Treats severe cold in the chest, inability to eat or drink, cold qi rising from the abdomen, pain above and below, sensitive to touch, with symptoms like a pale yellow complexion.
    Ingredients:

    • Two taels of ginseng
    • Two he (a unit of measurement) of Sichuan pepper, roasted to remove moisture
    • Four taels of dried ginger

    Combine the three ingredients with four sheng (a unit of measurement) of water, boil until two sheng remain, then strain. Add one sheng of syrup and simmer over low heat to extract one and a half sheng. Divide into two doses to take warm. If one can eat warm congee, cover it after cooking.

    Qi Shao Gui Ku Wine Decoction: Treats yellow sweat, with sweat soaking clothes like yellow herb juice.
    Ingredients:

    • Five taels of astragalus
    • Three taels each of white peony root and cinnamon twig

    Combine the three ingredients with one sheng of bitter wine and seven sheng of water, boil to obtain three sheng. Take one sheng warm. For vexation, take for six or seven days until relieved. If vexation persists, it is due to obstruction from the bitter wine.

    Cinnamon Twig Decoction with Astragalus: Treats jaundice with a floating pulse and harmonious abdomen; should induce sweating. If there is fullness in the abdomen with vomiting desire, and discomfort, it is better to induce vomiting instead of sweating.
    Ingredients:

    • Three taels each of cinnamon twig, white peony root, and fresh ginger
    • Twelve dates
    • Two taels each of astragalus and licorice

    Combine the six ingredients with eight sheng of water, boil to obtain three sheng. Take one sheng warm. Afterward, drink about one sheng of hot thin congee to enhance the medicinal effect and induce slight sweating. If there is no sweating, take more.[57p]

    　　黄芪汤 【《济生方》】 　治黄汗身体肿，发热不渴，汗出染衣黄色。　　黄芪蜜炙　赤芍药　茵陈各二两　石膏四两　麦门冬　淡豆豉各一两　甘草炙，半两　　右(口父)咀，每服四钱，水一盏，生姜五片，煎七分，去滓，食前服。一方入竹叶十四片，不用姜。一方无甘草。

    Huangqi Decoction [from "Jisheng Fang"]
    Treats yellow sweat, body swelling, fever without thirst, and sweat staining clothes yellow.

    Treats damp jaundice and difficulties in urination.

    Gu Dan Wan [from "Jisheng"]
    Treats food-related jaundice.
    Kushen, 3 taels; Longdancao, 1 tael; one cow gallbladder, extract the juice.
    Grind the above into a fine powder, using cow gall juice and a little refined honey, form into pills the size of a tung seed. Take 50 pills with warm boiled water or broth made from ginger and licorice. Taking with red pills is also acceptable.[58p]

    Huo Pi Decoction for Treating Jaundice
    Ingredients: fragrant leaves, loquat leaves (hairs removed), white mulberry bark, dried tangerine peel, kudzu root, white poria, chicken's foot seed, all in equal parts. Boil with water and add yellow minus pill.

    Angelica and Atractylodes Decoction [from "Three Causes Formula"] for Treating Jaundice.
    Ingredients: angelica, scutellaria, artemisia capillaris, roasted licorice (each 3g), poria, atractylodes (each 6g), half summer decoction soaked, peeled, roasted almonds, roasted orange peel, and roasted fish mint (each 4.5g). Boil with 480ml water and 3 slices of ginger until reduced to 240ml, then take after meals.

    Atractylodes Decoction for treating jaundice transforming into black jaundice, with symptoms of dark eyes and complexion, a feeling in the heart like eating raw garlic, black stools, numb skin, and pulse that is weak and rapid.
    Ingredients: atractylodes, cinnamon (each 3g), roasted orange peel, fermented soybean, dried kudzu, roasted almonds, roasted licorice (each 2.5g). Boil with 240ml water and reduce to 170ml, take before meals.

    Niter Powder [Zhong Jing] for treating black jaundice.
    Ingredients: niter and alum, both in equal parts. Burn the two ingredients to a powder. Mix with barley porridge juice and take a spoonful, three times a day. The illness will resolve with urination and defecation. Normal urine should be yellow, and normal stools should be black, indicating progress.

    　　肾疸汤 【东垣】 　治肾疸，目黄，浑身金色，小便赤濇。　　升麻根半两　苍朮一钱　防风根　独活根　白朮　柴胡根　羌活根　干葛根各半钱　白茯苓　猪苓　泽泻　甘草根各三钱　人参　神曲各六分　黄蘗二分　　分作二贴，水煎，食前稍热服。

    Talcum Powder for treating women's labor jaundice.

    One and a half liang of Talcum, one liang of Alumen, dried.

    Grind the above finely. Take two qian each time, mix with barley porridge before meals, according to urination producing yellow water. This is indeed the previous Nitrate formulation. The character for nitrate is similar to that of talcum; it is unknown which is correct, so keep both.

    Kidney Jaundice Decoction [from Dongyuan] for treating kidney jaundice, yellowing of the eyes, golden complexion throughout, and red and scanty urination.

    Half a liang of Stem of Transient Asarum, one qian each of Atractylodes, Saposhnikovia Root, Ligusticum Root, White Atractylodes, Bupleurum Root, Archangelica Root, and Pueraria Root; each half a qian; three qian each of White Poria, Zhu Ling, Ze Xie, and Licorice Root; six fen of Ginseng and Spirit Ferment; two fen of Coptis.     Poria Draining Dampness Decoction [from Baojian] for treating jaundice with chills and fever, vomiting, thirst with a desire to drink water, yellowing of the body and face, difficulty urinating, no appetite, and inability to lie down.

    Seven fen of Artemisia, six fen of White Poria, five fen each of Wood Poria, Ze Xie, White Atractylodes, Dried Citrus Peel, and Atractylodes rinsed and fried; four fen each of Fried Gardenia, Gentiana, and Stephania.

    Use two zhongs of water, boil down to seven fen, and take before meals.[61p]

    　　参朮健脾汤　治发黄日久，脾胃虚弱，饮食少思。　　人参　白朮各一钱五分　白茯苓　陈皮　白芍药煨　当归酒洗，各一钱　炙甘草七分　　水二锺，枣二枚，煎八分，食前服。色疸，加黄芪、炒白扁豆各一钱。
    　　当归秦艽散　治五疸，口淡咽干，倦怠，发热微寒。　　白朮　茯苓　秦艽　当归　川芎　白芍药　熟地黄酒蒸　陈皮留白，各一钱　半夏曲　炙甘草各五分　　水二锺，姜三片，煎八分，食前服。《济生》有肉桂、小草，名秦艽饮子。
    　　麻黄醇酒汤 【仲景】 　治黄疸。　　麻黄三两
    　　以好清酒五斤，煮取二升五合，顿服尽。冬月用酒煮，春月用水煮。
    　　黄连散 【《宝鉴》，下同】 　治黄疸，大小便闭濇壅热，累效。　　黄连　大黄酢炒，各二两　黄芩　甘草炙，各一两　　右为细末，食后温水调下二钱，日三服。先用瓜蒂散(口畜)鼻，滴出黄水，却服此药。[62p]

    Ginseng and Atractylodes Powder
    Treats long-term yellowing, weakened spleen and stomach, and little appetite.
    Ginseng, Atractylodes (each 1.5 grams), White Poria, tangerine peel, white peony root (stewed), and Angelica (each 1 gram), honey-fried licorice (0.7 grams).
    With 400 ml of water, add 2 dates, decoct to 240 ml, and take before meals. For jaundice, add Astragalus and fried white hyacinth bean (each 1 gram).

    Angelica and Gentian Powder
    Treats five types of jaundice, dry mouth and throat, fatigue, mild fever, and chills.
    Atractylodes, Poria, Gentian, Angelica, Chuanxiong, white peony root, and steamed prepared rhubarb (each 1 gram), half summer melon ferment, honey-fried licorice (each 0.5 grams).
    With 400 ml of water and 3 slices of ginger, decoct to 240 ml, and take before meals. In "Jisheng," there are cinnamon and small root, called Gentian Drinking Formula.

    Ephedra and Pure Wine Decoction (Zhongjing)
    Treats jaundice.
    Ephedra (6 grams) boiled with 2.5 liters of good clear wine, taken all at once. Use wine for winter and water for spring.

    Coptis Powder (from "Treasury")
    Treats jaundice, urinary and bowel obstruction, stagnation and heat.
    Coptis and rhubarb (each 60 grams), scutellaria and honey-fried licorice (each 30 grams).
    Grind to a fine powder, take 6 grams after meals mixed with warm water, three times a day. First use melon stem powder (mouth stock) to drip out yellow water, then take this medicine.[62p]

    　　(口畜)鼻瓜蒂散　治黄疸，浑身如金色。　　瓜蒂二钱　母丁香一钱　黍米四十九粒　赤小豆五分　　右为细末，每服临卧时先含水一口，却于两鼻孔(口畜)上半字便睡。至明日，取下黄水，便服黄连散。病轻者五日效，重者半月效。
    　　茵陈附子干姜汤　治寒湿相合，阴证发黄。　　茵陈一钱二分　附子炮去皮脐　白茯苓　橘红各三钱　干姜炮，二钱　草豆蔻煨，一两　白朮四分　枳实麸炒　半夏制　泽泻各半钱　　右生姜五片，水煎去滓，凉服。

    　　秦艽汤　一名秦艽散。治阴黄不欲闻人言，小便不利。　　秦艽一两　旋覆花　赤茯苓　炙甘草銼，各半两　　右(口父)咀，每服四钱，以牛乳汁一盏，煎至六分，去滓，不拘时温服。[63p]

    (Nasal Gourd Seed Powder) Treats jaundice, the body appearing golden. Gourd seeds: two qian, mother clove: one qian, millet: forty-nine grains, red beans: five fen. Grind everything into a fine powder. Before sleeping, take a mouthful of water and hold it, then place it at the upper half of both nostrils and sleep. By the next day, remove the yellow fluid and then take Huanglian Powder. For mild cases, it will be effective in five days; for severe cases, in half a month.

    Yinchen Fuzi Ginger Decoction Treats the combination of cold and dampness, with yin patterns causing yellowing. Yinchen: one qian and two fen, Fuzi (prepared and peeled): three qian, Bai Fuling: three qian, Citrus reticulata: three qian, dried ginger (prepared): two qian, grass cardamom (roasted): one liang, Bai Zhu: four fen, Zhi Shi (stir-fried): half a qian, Ban Xia (processed): half a qian, Ze Xie: half a qian. Use five slices of fresh ginger, decoct with water, remove dregs, and cool before taking.

    Qinjiao Decoction Also known as Qinjiao Powder. Treats yin jaundice where the patient does not wish to hear others speak, with difficulty in urination. Qinjiao: one liang, Xuanfu Hua: half a liang, red Poria: half a liang, roasted licorice: half a liang. Grind together; each dose is four qian, mixed with one cup of cow's milk, decoct until reduced to one-tenth, remove dregs, and take warm at any time.[63p]

    　　针砂丸 【《正传》】 　治谷疸酒疸，湿热发黄等证。　　针砂炒红酢淬，八两　香附子童便制　苍朮各四两　神曲炒　茵陈姜汁炒　麦芽炒，各二两　芍药　当归　生地黄　川芎　青皮各一两半　三棱　蓬朮并酢煮　陈皮各一两　栀子炒　姜黄　升麻　干漆炒，各五钱　　右为末，酢糊和为丸梧子大。姜汤下六七十丸。
    　　栀子蘗皮汤　治伤寒及湿家发黄。
    　　栀子十五枚　甘草一两　黄蘗二两
    　　水四升，煮取一升半，去滓，分温再服。
    　　大茵陈汤　治黄疸及头汗出欲发黄。　　茵陈蒿半两　大黄三钱　肥栀子三枚半　　水三升三合半，先煮茵陈减一半，内二味，煮取一升，去滓，分三服。小便利如皂角汁，一宿腹减，黄从小便中出也。
    　　茵陈栀子黄连三物汤　治大便自利而黄。　　茵陈蒿三钱　栀子　黄连各二钱
    　　水二盏，煎八分，去滓服。[64p]

    Zhen Sha Wan - Treats jaundice from grains, wine, and damp-heat causing yellowing.

    Ingredients:

    • Zhen Sha (1 tael)
    • Fried red vinegar (8 taels)
    • Xiang Fu (4 taels)
    • Tong Bian (4 taels)
    • Cang Zhu (4 taels)
    • Shen Qu (2 taels)
    • Yin Chen (2 taels)
    • Ginger juice (2 taels)
    • Malt (2 taels)
    • Shao Yao (1.5 taels)
    • Dang Gui (1.5 taels)
    • Sheng Di Huang (1.5 taels)
    • Chuan Xiong (1.5 taels)
    • Qing Pi (1.5 taels)
    • San Leng (1 tael)
    • Peng Zhu (1 tael)
    • Both vinegar boiled Chen Pi (1 tael)
    • Fried Zhi Zi (0.5 taels)
    • Jiang Huang (0.5 taels)
    • Sheng Ma (0.5 taels)
    • Gan Qi (0.5 taels)

    Grind these into a powder, mix with vinegar to form pills the size of a walnut. Take 60-70 pills with ginger soup.

    Zhi Zi-Ban Zhi Tang - Treats typhoid fever and dampness causing yellowing.

    Ingredients:

    • Zhi Zi (15 pieces)
    • Gan Cao (1 tael)
    • Huang Lian (2 taels)

    Add 4 sheng of water, boil down to 1.5 sheng, strain, and take warm in divisions.

    Da Yin Chen Tang - Treats jaundice and excessive sweating on the head leading to yellowing.

    Ingredients:

    • Yin Chen (0.5 taels)
    • Da Huang (0.3 taels)
    • Fat Zhi Zi (3.5 pieces)

    Add 3.5 sheng of water, first boil Yin Chen down to half, then add the other ingredients and boil to 1 sheng, strain and take in three servings. If bowel movements are easy, it indicates proper discharge of yellow through urine.

    Yin Chen Zhi Zi Huang Lian San - Treats diarrhea with yellowing.

    Ingredients:

    • Yin Chen (0.3 taels)
    • Zhi Zi (0.2 taels)
    • Huang Lian (0.2 taels)

    Add 2 cups of water, boil down to 80%, strain and take.[64p]

    　　山茵陈散　治疸证发热，大小便秘濇。　　山茵陈　栀子各二钱　赤茯　枳实各一钱半　葶苈　甘草各一钱　　右作一服，水二锺，姜三片，煎一锺，食前服。
    　　小温中丸 【丹溪，下同】 　治黄胖，宜草野贫贱人服，盖其饮食无积，但补阴燥湿而已。　　针砂一斤，以酢炒为末，入糯米一斤，炒极黄　　右为末，酢糊丸如桐子大，每米饮下四五十丸，忌口。轻者服五两，重者不过七两愈。
    　　大温中丸　治黄胖。丹溪晚年定者。　　香附童便浸，春夏一宿，秋冬三宿　针砂炒红酢淬三次，各一斤　苦参春夏二两，秋冬一两　芍药　厚朴姜制黑　山楂　苍朮泔浸，各五两　白朮　陈皮　茯苓各三两　青皮六两　甘草二两　　右为细末，酢糊丸如桐子大。面黑筋骨露气实者，米饮下五六十丸。面肥白与气虚羸弱者，白朮汤下三四十丸。忌一切生冷油腻鸡鹅羊鸭生硬并糍粽难化之物。服过七日后，便觉手掌心凉，口唇内有红晕起，调理半月愈。[65p]

    Shanyinchen Decoction
    For treating jaundice with fever, and constipation.
    Ingredients: Shanyinchen and Gardenia, each 2 qian; Red Poria and Bitter Orange, each 1.5 qian; Luffa and Licorice, each 1 qian.
    Prepare one dose with two sheng of water, three slices of ginger, boil down to one sheng, and take before meals.

    Xiaowenzhong Pill (by Danxi, same below)
    For treating yellow obesity; suitable for poor rural individuals, as their diet does not accumulate but only requires replenishing yin, drying dampness.
    One jin of needle sand, ground after frying in vinegar, combined with one jin of glutinous rice, fried until very yellow.
    Make into pills the size of a jujube, take four to fifty pills with rice drink, avoiding specific foods. Take five liang for mild cases and no more than seven liang for severe cases for recovery.

    Dawenzhong Pill
    For treating yellow obesity. This formula was finalized by Danxi in his later years.
    Soak Cyperus in boy's urine overnight in spring and summer, and for three nights in autumn and winter. Fry one jin of needle sand until red and steep in vinegar three times; for Kunbu, 2 liang in spring and summer, and 1 liang in autumn and winter; for Peony, Magnolia, Ginger processed with black, Hawthorn, and Atractylodes, each 5 liang; for White Atractylodes, Dried Tangerine Peel, and Poria, each 3 liang; for Green Peel, 6 liang; and for Licorice, 2 liang.
    Grind finely, make into pills the size of a jujube.
    For those with a dark complexion and exposed sinews, take five to sixty pills with rice drink. For those with a pale complexion and weak qi, take thirty to forty pills with White Atractylodes decoction. Avoid all raw, cold, oily, fatty foods including chicken, goose, lamb, duck, hard-to-digest items, and glutinous rice dumplings. After seven days of taking, one will notice cooling in the palms and lips showing a flush; regulating for half a month leads to recovery.[65p]

    　　右为末，每二钱，大麦粥饮调下。

    Nuanzhong Pill: Treats jaundice, dispels liver evils, and soothes spleen qi. Not suitable for the weak.
    Ingredients: 1 pound of Xiangfu, 2 taels of licorice, 10 taels of powdered gypsum, stir-fried until red, and soaked in vinegar. 5 qian each of dried tangerine peel, Atractylodes, magnolia bark, sparganium, white Atractylodes, and green skin.
    Grind to a fine powder, form into pills with vinegar paste, take 50 pills with empty stomach and ginger salt soup, or before dinner with wine. Avoid dog meat.

    Gypsum Powder (from "Qianjin Fang"): Treats jaundice in women, with yellowing of skin and blackening of the forehead, fever in the afternoon, urgency in the lower abdomen, and heat in the feet.
    Ingredients: Gypsum and talc in equal parts.
    Grind to a fine powder, take 2 qian mixed with barley porridge.

    Qinjiao Drink (from "Deyao"): Treats jaundice in women.
    Ingredients: 1 qian each of Qinjiao, Angelica, Peony, White Atractylodes, cinnamon, red Poria, dried tangerine peel, cooked Rehmannia, Chuanxiong; 5 fen each of Pinellia and licorice.
    Grind, prepare into a paste, add 5 slices of ginger, and decoct in water for consumption.

    Yinchen Da Huang Decoction (from "Huoren Shu", applies here): Treats exogenous cold with great heat and jaundice.
    Ingredients: 1 qian each of Yinchen, gardenia, Bupleurum, Coptis, Scutellaria, Cimicifuga, and rhubarb; 5 fen of gentian.
    Decoct in water for consumption.[66p]

    Yinchen Zhi Zi Decoction: Treats jaundice from excess bile.
    Ingredients: 3 qian Yinchen, 2 qian Dahuang, 1 qian each of Zhizi and Zhishi. Decoction with water.

    Yinchen Fuling Decoction: Treats damp-heat jaundice with difficulty in urination, agitation, and thirst.
    Ingredients: 3 qian Yinchen, 1 qian each of Baifuling, Zhuling, Huashi, Danggui, and Guigen. Decoction with water.

    Yinchen Jupi Decoction: Treats damp-heat jaundice with agitation, cough, and no thirst.
    Ingredients: 1 qian each of Yinchen, Chenpi, Baizhu, Shengjiang, Banxia, and Fuling. Decoction with water.

    Yinchen Fuzi Decoction: Treats damp-heat jaundice with coldness all over.
    Ingredients: 1 qian each of Yinchen, prepared Fuzi, and roasted Gancao. Decoction with water.

    Ingredients: 1 qian each of Yinchen, prepared Fuzi, and prepared Ganjiang. Decoction with water.

    Ingredients: 1 qian each of Yinchen, Wuzhuyu, prepared Fuzi, prepared Ganjiang, Muti, and Danggui. Decoction with water.[67p]

    　　瘴疸丸 【《入门》】 　治天行病急黄，及瘴疟发黄。　　茵陈　栀子　大黄　芒硝各一两　杏仁六钱　常山　鳖甲　巴豆霜各四钱　豆豉二钱　　右为末，蒸饼和丸梧子大。每三丸或五丸，温水吞下，以吐利为效。《得效方》栀子丸同，即今茵陈丸也。

    　　退黄散 【《医鉴》】 　治黄疸身面如金，小便如黄蘗汁。　　柴胡　升麻　草龙胆　茵陈　黄连　黄芩　栀子　黄蘗　木通　滑石各一钱　甘草五分　　右銼，作一贴，灯心一握，水煎服。[68p]

    Zhàngdǎn Wán (Zhuangdan Pill) - Treats acute yellowing from climatic diseases and yellowing from malaria. Ingredients: 1 tael of Yīnchén, Zhīzǐ, Dàhuáng, Mángxiāo; 6 qian of Xìngrén; 4 qian each of Chángshān, Biējiǎ, Bādòu shuāng; 2 qian of Dòuchǐ. Grind into powder, form into pills the size of a jujube. Take 3 or 5 pills with warm water, aiming for purging effects. The Zhīzǐ Wán is the same as this and is now known as Yīnchén Wán.

    Yīnchén Xièhuáng Tāng (Yinchen Decoction for Reducing Yellow) - Treats seasonal fevers leading to yellow jaundice, known as epidemic jaundice. Ingredients: 1.5 qian of Gégēn; 7 fen of Mùxiāng; 1 qian each of Yīnchén, Huánglián (stir-fried), Zhīzǐ (stir-fried), Bái zhú, Chìfúlíng, Sháoyào, Hòubǎn, Mùtōng, Rénshēn. Shred, prepare into a patch, with 3 slices of ginger, decoct in water for consumption.

    Jìshēng Yīnchén Tāng (Jisheng Yinchen Decoction) - Treats seasonal heat stagnation causing general yellowing. Ingredients: 4 qian of Yīnchén, 2 qian of Dàhuáng, 1 qian of Zhīzǐ. Shred, prepare into a patch, and decoct in water for consumption.

    Tuìhuáng Sǎn (Yellow Reducing Powder) - Treats jaundice with a golden appearance of the body and face, and urine resembling yellow bile. Ingredients: 1 qian each of Chái hú, Shēng má, Cǎo lóngdǎn, Yīnchén, Huánglián, Huángqín, Zhīzǐ, Huángbò, Mùtōng, Shuíshí; 5 fen of Gāncǎo. Shred, prepare into a patch, combine with a fistful of lantern heart (the pith of the lotus stem), decoct in water for consumption.[68p]

    　　退黄丸 【《入门》】 　治黄疸水肿，腹胀溏泄等证。　　青矾二两，锅内镕化，入陈黄米四升，用酢拌匀，慢火炒令烟尽，入平胃散六两同炒，少顷去火毒　　右为末，酢糊丸梧子大。每七十丸，空心临卧米饮下。忌糯米油面生冷硬物。此方即周益公阴隲丸，盖青矾乃铜之精液，用酢制以平肝，愈于针砂。如服针砂，不忌盐，后复发。青矾则不忌盐，不复发。
    　　褪金丸 【《正传》】 　治黄肿绝妙。　　针砂煅红醉淬　香附子便浸，各六两　苍朮　白朮各二两半　陈皮　神曲　麦芽各一两半　厚朴　甘草各一两　　右为末，曲糊和丸梧子大。米饮下五七十丸。忌鱼腥湿面生冷。有块加三棱、蓬朮，并酢煮各两半。
    　　绿矾丸 【《正传》】 　治黄肿病最捷。　　五倍炒黑　神曲炒黄，各八两　针砂炒红酢淬　绿矾姜汁炒白，各四两　　右为末，姜汁煮枣肉，捣丸梧子大。温酒下六七十丸。不饮酒，米饮下。终身忌食荞麦，犯之再发难治。[69p]

    Tui Huang Wan
    Treats jaundice, water retention, abdominal distension, and diarrhea.
    Two taels of blue vitriol, melted in a pot, mix in four sheng of aged yellow rice, stir with vinegar until well combined, then sauté over low heat until the smoke dissipates. Add six taels of Pingwei San and sauté together for a while, then remove the fire to eliminate toxins.
    Grind this mixture into a powder, then form into pills the size of a large jujube. Take seventy pills, taken on an empty stomach with rice drink when lying down. Avoid sticky rice, oily wheat flour, raw cold hard foods. This recipe is the Yin Zhi Wan from Zhou Yigong; blue vitriol is a refined essence of copper, prepared with vinegar to calm the liver, curing better than with needle sand. If taking needle sand, do not avoid salt; if salt is consumed, it will relapse. However, with blue vitriol, there is no need to avoid salt, and it will not relapse.

    Tui Jin Wan
    An excellent remedy for jaundice and swelling.
    Prepare six taels each of needle sand, roasted red then quenched, and cyperus, soaked. Also, prepare two and a half taels each of Atractylodes, white Atractylodes, one and a half taels each of aged tangerine peel, Shenchuan, and malt, along with one tael each of Magnolia bark and licorice.
    Grind this mixture into a powder, mix with a paste made from the combined ingredients into pills sized like a large jujube. Take fifty to seventy pills with rice drink. Avoid fishy, wet foods, raw cold items. Optional additions include two and a half taels each of euphorbia and Atractylodes, boiled in vinegar.

    Lu Fan Wan
    The fastest treatment for jaundice and swelling.
    Eight taels each of roasted black five-fold, and roasted yellow Shenchuan. Four taels each of needle sand, roasted red and quenched, green vitriol, and ginger juice.
    Grind this mixture into a powder, and make pills using ginger juice boiled with jujube pulp, forming them into the size of large jujubes. Take sixty to seventy pills with warm wine. If avoiding alcohol, take with rice drink. For a lifetime, avoid buckwheat; if consumed, it will be difficult to treat again.[69p]

    　　疸方 【《入门》，下同】 　治黄疸，爱吃茶叶者。　　苍朮　白朮各三两　石膏　白芍药　黄芩　南星　陈皮各一两　薄荷七钱　　右为末，砂糖水煮，神曲作糊，和丸梧子大。砂糖水，空心吞下五七十丸。　　又方　治黄疸，喜吃生米者。
    　　白朮一钱半　苍朮一钱三分　白芍药　陈皮　神曲　麦芽　山楂肉　白茯苓　石膏各一钱　厚朴七分　藿香五分　甘草三分　　右銼，作一贴，水煎，临熟入砂糖末一匙，调服。
    　　四宝丹　治疸癖爱吃土、炭、生米、茶叶，通用者。　　使君子肉二两　南星姜制　槟榔各一两　　如吃生米，加麦芽一斤炒过；吃茶叶，加茶叶一斤炒过；吃土，加壁土一斤炒过；吃炭，加黑炭一斤炒过。共为末，蜜丸梧子大，空心，砂糖水下五十丸。[70p]

    Jaundice Formula
    To treat jaundice, for those who love to eat tea leaves.

    • 3 taels of Cangzhu
    • 3 taels of Baizhu
    • 1 tael each of Gypsum, Baishao, Huangqin, Nanxing, Chenpi
    • 7 qian of Mint

    Grind these ingredients into a powder, boil with sugar water, and make a paste with Shenqu. Form into pills the size of a walnut. Swallow 50 to 70 pills with sugar water on an empty stomach.

    Another Formula
    To treat jaundice for those who enjoy eating raw rice.

    • 1.5 qian of Baizhu
    • 1.3 qian of Cangzhu
    • 1 qian each of Baishao, Chenpi, Shenqu, Malts, Hawthorn flesh, Baifuling, Gypsum
    • 7 fen of Houpu
    • 5 fen of Huo香
    • 3 fen of Gancao

    Grate these ingredients to make one dose. Brew with water, and when nearly done, add a spoonful of sugar to adjust the flavor for consumption.

    Four Treasures Pill
    To treat stubborn jaundice for those who love to eat dirt, charcoal, raw rice, or tea leaves; this is a general formula.

    • 2 taels of Sishenjizi (areca nut)
    • 1 tael each of Nanxing and processed Ginger
    • 1 tael of Betel nut

    If eating raw rice, add 1 jin of roasted malt; if tea leaves, add 1 jin of roasted tea leaves; if dirt, add 1 jin of wall soil; if charcoal, add 1 jin of black charcoal. Grind all into a powder, form into honey pills the size of a walnut, and swallow 50 pills with sugar water on an empty stomach.[70p]

    　　逍遥散 【《元戎》】 　治湿郁发黄。　　当归　芍药　白朮　茯神　甘草　柴胡各等分　　右，姜三片，水煎服。

    Xiaoyao San 【from "Yuan Rong"】
    Used for dampness and jaundice.
    Each of the following in equal parts: Angelica, Peony, Atractylodes, Poria, Licorice, Bupleurum.
    Add three slices of ginger, decoct in water and take.

    Hong Wan Zi 【from "He Ji"】
    Used for jaundice due to food.
    Soak and slice three pounds of Radix Sparganii, and five pounds each of Atractylodes and Chen Pi (dried tangerine peel), removing the white.
    Roast three pounds of dried ginger and three pounds of black pepper.
    Grind all ingredients into a fine powder, mix with vinegar dough to form pills the size of walnut seeds, coated with red alum.
    Take thirty pills after meals, with ginger soup. Adjust dosage for children as needed.

    Liu Wei Di Huang Wan
    Used for all types of kidney water deficiency, and also treats yin deficiency jaundice.
    Eight taels of cooked Rehmannia, steamed and mashed; four taels each of Cornus and Dioscorea, toasted; three taels each of Moutan Root, Alisma, and white Poria.
    Grind into a fine powder, mix with Rehmannia paste, and add honey to form pills the size of walnut seeds.
    Take seventy to eighty pills before meals with plain white soup or mild salt soup.
    Add one tael each of cinnamon and processed Aconite for a variant called Ba Wei Wan, which treats symptoms of yin and yang deficiency.[71p]

    Yigong San: Treats deficiency and cold of the spleen and stomach, characterized by little appetite, vomiting with yellow fluid, or cough with a puffy face, upward qi, abdominal fullness, and similar symptoms. Ingredients: Ginseng, fried Atractylodes, Poria, honey-fried Licorice, and Chen Pi, each one qian (approximately 3 grams). Add ginger and jujube, decoct in water and take.

    Ge Hua Jie Cheng Tang (by Dong Yuan): Treats alcohol-related jaundice. Ingredients: Ginseng, Atractylodes, white Poria, cardamom, white cardamom, and Ge Hua (Kudzu flower), each one qian; Shen Qu and Mu Xiang, each five fen (approximately 1.5 grams); Qing Pi, Chen Pi, Zhu Ling, and Ze Xie, each seven fen. Use two chong of water, five slices of fresh ginger, decoct to seven parts, take warm after meals, induce slight sweating to alleviate alcohol-related issues; alternatively, grind into powder and take two to three qian with ginger vinegar soup.

    Ru Shen San (from "De Xiao" text): Treats alcohol toxicity resulting in jaundice. Ingredients: Bitter melon seeds and bitter cucumber seeds, each thirty-seven; three hundred grains of yellow millet; two pieces of benzoin resin. Grind to powder, take a considerable amount (as advised) into the nose to stop yellow discharge. If excessive, use some ash from millet and a small amount of musk powder in the nose to stop immediately.[72p]

    Gypsum and Artemisia Decoction
    Treats jaundice with the entire body turning yellow and hunger appearing immediately after eating.
    Ingredients: 2 qian of gypsum, 0.5 qian of licorice, 1 qian each of gardenia seeds, artemisia, akebia, and rhubarb, and one fruit of the loquat.
    Crush the above ingredients into a powder, prepare a dose, add 5 slices of ginger and 2 green onions, then boil in water to take.

    Guaranteed Effect Powder
    Commonly used for jaundice.
    Ingredients: 1 qian each of stir-fried fine lepidium, gentian, gardenia, and scutellaria, and 2 qian of artemisia.
    Crush the above ingredients into a powder, prepare a dose, and boil in water to take.

    Poria Modified Decoction
    Treats biliary heat accumulation in the stomach with hunger appearing immediately after eating, yellow and thin face, fullness in the chest and swelling in the sides, and red, difficult urination.
    Ingredients: 3 liang of red poria, aged tangerine peel (white part removed), and mulberry root bark; 4 liang of red peony and white atractylodes; 2 liang each of ginseng and cinnamon, 8 liang of gypsum, and 6 liang of pinellia (washed, with fresh ginger for roasting).
    Grind into a powder, take 3 qian with 1 cup of water and 10 slices of fresh ginger, boil until reduced to 80% without regard to the time. If the illness is severe, add 2 liang each of rhubarb and glauber's salt.

    Jujube and Green Vitriol Pill
    Treats jaundice obesity disease.
    Ingredients: 1 liang each of calcined needle sand and green vitriol, stir-fried; 1 liang each of white atractylodes, magnolia bark, aged tangerine peel, and medicated leaven; 0.5 liang of licorice.
    Grind into a powder, steam jujube meat, mix and form pills the size of a wutong nut. Take 50 to 70 pills with rice drink. Avoid buckwheat, lamb, and pork from sows as they can cause immediate death without medical help.[73p]

    　　五疸(口畜)鼻方 【《千金》，下同】 　通治五疸。　　瓜蒂　秫米　赤小豆各二七枚
    　　右三味，治下筛，病重者取如大豆二枚，内着鼻孔中，痛缩鼻，须臾当出黄汁。或从口中出汁升余则愈。　　病轻者如一豆。不瘥，间日复用。又下里间以筒使人吹鼻中，无不死，大慎之。《删繁》疗天时毒热，通贯脏腑，沉伏骨髓之间，或为黄疸、黑疸、赤疸、白疸、谷疸、马黄等病，喘息须臾不绝也。

    Wudan (Five Jaundices) Nose Recipe
    This recipe treats the five types of jaundice.

    Ingredients:

    • Gourd stems: 27 pieces
    • Sorghum rice: 27 pieces
    • Red beans: 27 pieces

    Preparation and Usage: Mix these three ingredients and process them. For severe cases, take two beans the size of soybeans and insert them into the nostrils; this will cause pain and constriction in the nose, and shortly thereafter, yellow fluid will emerge. Alternatively, the fluid may expel from the mouth, leading to recovery. For lighter cases, use only one bean. If the condition does not improve, repeat in intervals of days. Additionally, use a tube to blow into the nose; there is no failure in treatment, but caution is advised.

    Dahuang Pill – Treats the preceding symptoms.
    Ingredients:

    • Dahuang (Rhubarb): 2 taels
    • Tengliazi (Cabbage seeds): 2 taels

    Preparation: Grind these ingredients into a powder, mix with honey, and form pills about the size of walnuts. Take ten pills each time, three times a day, and stop when the illness is resolved.

    Wudan Recipe
    Ingredients:

    • Dahuang (Rhubarb): 2 taels
    • Huanglian (Coptis root): 3 taels
    • Huangbo (Phellodendron bark): 1 tael
    • Huangqin (Scutellaria root): 1 tael
    • Quyi (Malted grain): 5 qian

    Preparation: Grind these five ingredients into a powder, mix with honey, and make pills the size of walnuts. Take three pills before meals, three times a day, and adjust up to five pills if necessary.[74p]

    　　三黄散　治黄疸，身体面目尽黄。
    　　大黄　黄连　黄芩各四两
    　　右三味，治下筛，先食，服方寸匕，日三。亦可为丸。
    　　秦椒散　治黄疸，饮少溺多。
    　　秦椒六铢　瓜蒂半两
    　　右二味，治下筛，水服方寸匕，日三。　　又方　治发黄，身面目悉黄如金色，小便如浓煮蘗汁，众医不能疗者。　　茵陈　栀子各四两　黄芩　大黄　柴胡　升麻各三两　龙胆二两　　右七味(口父)咀，以水八升，煮取二升七合，分三服。若身体羸者，加大黄、栀子五六两，生地黄一升。如黄发已久，变作桃皮色，心下有坚，呕逆不下饮食，小便急，赤色少，四肢逆冷，脉深沉极微细迟者，不宜服此方，服下必变啘也。宜与大茵陈汤，除大黄与生地黄五两，服汤尽。消息看脉小浮出形小见，不甚沉微，便可治也。脉浮见者，黄当明，不复作桃皮色，心下自宽也。[75p]

    San Huang San treats jaundice, causing the body and face to turn completely yellow.

    Ingredients:

    • Da Huang (Rhubarb) 4 taels
    • Huang Lian (Coptis) 4 taels
    • Huang Qin (Scutellaria) 4 taels

    Mix these three ingredients. For treatment, take a spoonful before meals, three times a day. It can also be made into pills.

    Qin Jiao San treats jaundice with little drinking and frequent urination.

    Ingredients:

    • Qin Jiao (Zanthoxylum) 6 zhū
    • Guā Tí (Melon Stem) 0.5 taels

    Mix these two ingredients. For treatment, take with water, using a spoonful three times a day.

    Another Formula treats jaundice, where the face and body appear completely yellow like gold, and urination resembles thick cooked plant juice, even when other doctors cannot treat it.

    Ingredients:

    • Yin Chen (Artemisia) 4 taels
    • Zhi Zi (Gardenia) 4 taels
    • Huang Qin (Scutellaria) 3 taels
    • Da Huang (Rhubarb) 3 taels
    • Chai Hu (Bupleurum) 3 taels
    • Sheng Ma (Cimicifuga) 3 taels
    • Long Dan (Gentian) 2 taels

    Crush these seven ingredients. Use 8 sheng of water, boil down to 2.7 sheng, and divide into three doses.

    If the body is weak, add 5-6 taels of Da Huang and Zhi Zi, and 1 sheng of Sheng Di (Rehmannia).

    If jaundice has lasted a long time and has turned into a peach skin color, with hardness below the heart, nausea preventing intake, urgent and scant red urine, cold extremities, and very weak shallow pulse, do not take this formula as it will worsen the condition. Instead, use Da Yin Chen Tang, omitting Da Huang and Sheng Di by 5 taels, and consume the entire decoction.

    Watch for the pulse; if it is slightly floating and palpable, treatment can proceed. If the pulse is floating, it indicates the yellow should clear and the complexion will return to normal, relieving the discomfort beneath the heart.[75p]

    Huangdantang (Jaundice Decoction) treats jaundice.
    Yinchen, Huangbai, Zhizhi, and Dahuang, each three taels; Huanglian. Combine these five ingredients, chew, then use nine sheng of water to boil and extract three sheng. Divide into three doses, taking the decoction first, then taking the pills afterward.

    Huangdanwan (Jaundice Pills) treats the above condition.
    Dahuang, five taels; Yinchen and Zhizhi, each three taels; Huangqin, Huangbai, and Huanglian, each two taels. Crush these six ingredients into powder, mix with honey to make pills the size of a wutong nut. Take twenty pills with warm water, which will promote slight bowel movements.

    Dahuang Huangbai Tang (Dahuang and Huangbai Decoction) treats jaundice, abdominal fullness, difficulty in urination with red urine, and spontaneous sweating. This indicates exterior harmony with internal fullness, requiring a purgative.
    Dahuang, three taels; Huangbai and Mangxiao, each four taels; Zhizhi, fifteen pieces. Crush these four ingredients, use six sheng of water to boil and extract two sheng. Remove the dregs, add Mangxiao back in, and boil again to extract one sheng. Take it before meals.[76p]

    　　茵陈丸　治时行病急黄，并瘴疠疫气及痎疟。　　茵陈　栀子　芒硝　杏仁各三两　巴豆一两　常山　鳖甲各二两　豆豉　大黄各五两　　右九味为末，以饧为丸如梧子大。饮服三丸，以吐利为佳，不知加一丸。初觉体气有异，急服之，即瘥。神效。
    　　急黄方　治急黄，热气骨蒸，两目赤脉。　　芒硝一两　大黄末两半　生地黄汁八合　　右三味合和，一服五合，日二，以利为度，不须二服。
    　　风疸方　治风疸，小便或黄或白，洒洒寒热，好卧不欲动。　　三月生艾一束，捣汁，铜器中煎，如漆密封之　苦参　大黄　黄连　凝水石研　(艹舌)蒌根　葶苈各六味　　右七味，六味为末，以艾煎和，丸如梧子大。先食服五丸，日二，可至二十丸。有热加苦参，渴加(艹舌)蒌，小便濇加葶苈，小便多加凝水石，小便白加黄连，大便难加大黄。[77p]

    Yin Chen Pill
    Treats epidemic jaundice with acute yellowing, as well as pestilential and epidemic qi, and intermittent fever.
    Ingredients:
    Yin Chen, Zhi Zi, Mang Xiao, and Xing Ren each 3 taels; Ba Dou 1 tael; Chang Shan and Bie Jia each 2 taels; Dou Chi and Da Huang each 5 taels.
    Grind these nine ingredients into a powder and form into pills the size of a wuzi (small nut). Take three pills, ideally to induce vomiting and relieve symptoms, but do not take more than one additional pill. If one first feels a change in bodily energy, take it promptly to recover. The effect is miraculous.

    Acute Jaundice Formula
    Treats acute jaundice with heat causing bone steaming and red eyes.
    Ingredients:
    Mang Xiao 1 tael; Da Huang powder 2.5 taels; Sheng Di Huang juice 8 jugs.
    Mix these three ingredients and take 5 jugs at a time, twice daily, adjusting based on the effect without needing to take two doses.

    Wind Jaundice Formula
    Treats wind jaundice with urine that may be yellow or white, experiencing chills and fevers, preferring to lie still.
    Ingredients:
    Three bundles of mugwort harvested in March, crushed for juice, boiled in a copper vessel sealed tightly; Ku Shen, Da Huang, Huang Lian, Ning Shui Shi powdered; (Cao She) Lou Gen; and Ting Li each 6 ingredients.
    Grind the 6 ingredients into a powder and combine with the mugwort juice to form pills the size of a wuzi. Take five pills before meals, up to twice daily, with a maximum of twenty pills. For heat symptoms, add Ku Shen; for thirst, add (Cao She) Lou; for thick urine, add Ting Li; for high frequency, add Ning Shui Shi; for white urine, add Huang Lian; for difficult bowel movements, add Da Huang.[77p]

    　　栀子枳实豉大黄汤　又名枳实大黄汤。治伤寒食少，饮多痰结，发黄酒疸，心中懊憹而不甚热，或干呕。　　枳实五枚　大黄三两　豆豉半升　栀子七枚　　右四味(口父)咀，以水六升，煮取二升，分三服。心中热疼懊憹皆主之。
    　　凝水石散　治肉疸，饮少，小便多，如白泔色，此病得之纵酒。　　凝水石　白石脂　(艹舌)蒌根　桂心各三十铢　菟丝子　知母各十八铢　　右六味，治下筛，麦粥饮服五钱匕，日三服。五日知，十日瘥。
    　　茯苓丸　治心下纵横坚而小便赤，是酒疸。　　半夏　杏仁各十八铢　蜀椒　当归各十二铢　甘遂六铢　茯苓　茵陈　干姜各一两　枳实　白朮熬，各三十铢　　右十味为末，蜜和丸如梧子大。空腹服三丸，日三。稍稍加，以小便利为度。《千金翼》加黄连二两，大黄十八铢，名茵陈丸，治黑疸身体暗黄，小便濇。[78p]

    Grapefruit and Rhubarb Decoction
    Also known as Grapefruit and Rhubarb Decoction. It treats symptoms of cold damage, decreased appetite, excessive phlegm, jaundice from alcohol, a feeling of vexation in the heart without intense heat, or dry retching.
    Ingredients:

    • 5 pieces of grapefruit
    • 6 taels of rhubarb
    • 0.5 sheng of fermented soybeans
    • 7 pieces of gardenia
      The above four ingredients should be crushed; with 6 sheng of water, boil to extract 2 sheng, and divide into three doses. This is indicated for heart heat pain and vexation.

    Condensed Water Stone Powder
    Treats biliary jaundice with decreased thirst and increased urination, presenting pale urine; this ailment arises from excessive drinking.
    Ingredients:

    • 30 zhu of Condensed Water Stone
    • 30 zhu of White Stone Fat
    • 30 zhu of Trichosanthes Root
    • 30 zhu of Cinnamon Heart
    • 18 zhu of Cuscuta Seed
    • 18 zhu of Anemarrhena
      The above six ingredients should be prepared into a powder. Take 5 qian mixed with millet porridge and drink three times a day. A recovery is expected within five to ten days.

    Poria Pills
    Used for hardness and constriction below the heart with red urination, indicating jaundice from alcohol.
    Ingredients:

    • 18 zhu of Pinellia
    • 18 zhu of Apricot Kernel
    • 12 zhu of Sichuan Pepper
    • 12 zhu of Angelica
    • 6 zhu of Euphorbia
    • 1 liang each of Poria, Artemisia, and Dried Ginger
    • 30 zhu of Grapefruit and 30 zhu of Atractylodes, boiled together
      The above ten ingredients should be ground into powder, mixed with honey to form pills the size of a walnut. Take three pills on an empty stomach, three times daily. Gradually increase the dosage until urination becomes more comfortable. According to Qianjin Yi, add 2 liang of Coptis and 18 zhu of rhubarb to create a formulation called Artemisia Pills, which treats black jaundice with dark yellow skin and turbid urination.[78p]

    　　半夏汤　治酒癖阴黄，胸心胀满，骨肉沉重，逆害饮食，乃至小便赤黄，此根本虚劳，风冷饮食冲心，由脾胃内痰所致。　　半夏一升　生姜　黄芩　茵陈　当归　前胡　枳实　甘草　大戟各二两　茯苓　白朮各三两　　右十一味(口父)咀，以水一斗，煮取三升，分作三服。
    　　牛胆丸　治酒疸，身黄曲尘出。
    　　牛胆一枚　芫花一升　荛花　大黄各半斤　瓜蒂三两　　右五味，四味(口父)咀，以清酒一斗渍一宿，煮减半，去滓，内牛胆，微火煎令可丸，如大豆，服一丸。日移六七尺不知，复一丸至八丸。膈上吐，膈下下，或不吐而自愈。[79p]

    Banxia Decoction: Treats alcohol addiction with symptoms of yellow discharges, chest fullness, heaviness in the bones and flesh, adverse reactions to food and drink, and red-yellow urination. This is fundamentally due to vacuity and fatigue, caused by wind and cold dietary elements affecting the heart, resulting from phlegm in the spleen and stomach. Ingredients include one sheng of Banxia, ginger, Huangqin, Yinchén, Danggui, Qianhu, Zhishi, and Dajue, each two liang; and three liang each of Fuling and Baizhu. Combine these eleven ingredients, pulverize, and boil with one dou of water to obtain three sheng, divided into three doses.

    Niudan Pill: Treats jaundice due to alcohol, with symptoms of yellow skin and feces resembling dust. Ingredients include one piece of ox gall, one sheng of Yanhua, half a jin each of Yao flower and Dahuang, and three liang of guati. Combine these five ingredients, pulverize four of them, soak in one dou of clear wine overnight, reduce by half through boiling, strain, add ox gall, and simmer on low heat until it can be formed into pills the size of soybeans. Take one pill, and if symptoms persist, take up to eight pills. The patient may experience vomiting above and purging below, or self-recovery without vomiting.[79p]

    　　大茵陈汤　治内实热盛发黄，黄如金色，脉浮大滑实紧数者。夫发黄多是酒客劳热食少，胃中热，或温毒内热者，故黄如金色。　　茵陈　黄蘗　大黄　白朮各三两　黄芩　甘草　茯苓　(艹舌)蒌根　前胡　枳实各二两　栀子二十枚　　右十一味(口父)咀，以水九升，煮取三升，分三服，得快下，消息三四日，更治之。
    　　茵陈丸　治气淋胪胀腹大，身体面目悉黄，及酒疸短气不得息。　　茵陈　天门冬　栀子各四两　半夏半升　大黄　桂心各三两　通草　石膏各二两　　右八味，蒸大黄、通草、天门冬、半夏、栀子，曝令干，合捣筛，蜜丸如大豆。服三丸，日三。忌生鱼。以豆羹服，不得用酒。一方，去石膏，内滑石二两。不知，加至十丸。
    　　犀角散 【《良方》】 　治急黄，心膈烦躁而渴者。　　犀角　黄连　升麻　栀子仁各一两　茵陈　　右(口父)咀，每服四钱，姜三片，水二锺，煎至六分，温服。[80p]

    Da Yin Chen Decoction: This treats internal excess heat manifesting as jaundice, with a yellow color like gold, and a pulse that is floating, large, slippery, solid, tight, and rapid. Jaundice is often due to excessive alcohol consumption, heat from labor, and insufficient food, resulting in heat in the stomach or from warm toxins. Hence, the yellow appears like gold.

    Ingredients:

    • Yin Chen: 3 taels
    • Huang Bai: 3 taels
    • Da Huang: 3 taels
    • Bai Zhu: 3 taels
    • Huang Qin: 2 taels
    • Gan Cao: 2 taels
    • Fu Ling: 2 taels
    • Lou Gen (reeds): 2 taels
    • Qian Hu: 2 taels
    • Zhi Shi: 2 taels
    • Zhi Zi: 20 pieces

    Combine the eleven ingredients, grind them, and boil in 9 liters of water until 3 liters remain. Divide into three doses, taking to relieve quickly. Observe for three to four days, then treat again.

    Yin Chen Pills: This treats urinary obstruction and abdominal swelling, with a yellow complexion and shortness of breath due to alcohol-induced jaundice.

    Ingredients:

    • Yin Chen: 4 taels
    • Tian Men Dong: 4 taels
    • Zhi Zi: 4 taels
    • Ban Xia: 1/2 sheng
    • Da Huang: 3 taels
    • Gui Xin: 3 taels
    • Tong Cao: 2 taels
    • Shi Gao: 2 taels

    Steam Da Huang, Tong Cao, Tian Men Dong, Ban Xia, and Zhi Zi until dry. Crush and sieve them, then mix into honey to form pills the size of soybeans. Take three pills, three times daily. Avoid raw fish and do not use alcohol. In another method, omit Shi Gao and add 2 taels of Shuai Shi instead. If unsure, take up to ten pills.

    Rhinoceros Horn Powder (from "Liang Fang"): This treats acute jaundice, accompanied by irritability and thirst.

    Ingredients:

    • Rhinoceros Horn: 1 tael
    • Huang Lian: 1 tael
    • Sheng Ma: 1 tael
    • Zhi Zi Ren: 1 tael
    • Yin Chen: 1 tael

    Grind these ingredients. For each dose, take 4 qian with three slices of ginger, and 2 cups of water. Boil down to two-thirds, and take warm.[80p]

    　　养劳汤 【《纲目》】 　治五疸，脚弱心忪，口淡耳聋，微寒发热，气急，小便白浊，当作虚劳治之。　　黄芪　当归　桂心　甘草炙　陈皮　白朮　人参各一两　白芍药三两　熟地　五味子　茯苓各三钱　远志去心，半两　　右每服四钱，姜枣煎，空心服。

    　　谷芽枳实小柴胡汤 【《良方》，下同】 　治谷疸，食已即饥，而头眩心中怫郁不安，饥饱所致，蒸熏而黄。　　谷芽　枳实　厚朴各一钱　山栀　大黄　柴胡　黄芩各六分　陈皮　半夏　人参　炙甘草各五分　　右，水二盏，姜三片，枣一枚，煎八分，不拘时服。
    　　紫金丹　治黄疸久不愈，胃强者。
    　　胆矾　黄蜡各二两　大枣五十枚
    　　右以砂锅或银石器内，用好酢三碗，先下矾枣，慢火熬，半日取出枣，去皮核，次下蜡，再熬一二时如膏，入蜡茶二两，同和丸桐子大。每服三十丸，茶酒任下。酒人下血色黄目黄色有余者，亦效。[81p]

    Yang Lao Tang
    For treating jaundice with symptoms such as weakness in the legs, anxiety in the heart, bland taste in the mouth, deafness, mild chills with fever, shortness of breath, and cloudy urine, it should be treated as deficiency and labor.
    Ingredients:

    • Astragalus 1 tael
    • Angelica 1 tael
    • Cinnamon heart 1 tael
    • Honey-fried licorice 1 tael
    • Dried tangerine peel 1 tael
    • White atractylodes 1 tael
    • Ginseng 1 tael
    • White peony 3 taels
    • Cooked rehmannia 3 qian
    • Schisandra 3 qian
    • Poria 3 qian
    • Polygala root (remove heart) ½ tael
      Each dose is 4 qian, boiled with ginger and jujube, taken on an empty stomach.

    Gu Ya Zhi Shi Xiao Chai Hu Tang
    For treating food-induced jaundice where hunger immediately follows eating, accompanied by dizziness, anxiety, and yellowing from steam and smoke.
    Ingredients:

    • Barley sprout 1 qian
    • Bitter orange 1 qian
    • Magnolia bark 1 qian
    • Gardenia 6 fen
    • Rhubarb 6 fen
    • Chai Hu (Bupleurum) 6 fen
    • Scutellaria 6 fen
    • Dried tangerine peel 5 fen
    • Pinellia 5 fen
    • Ginseng 5 fen
    • Honey-fried licorice 5 fen
      Use 2 cups of water, 3 slices of ginger, and 1 jujube, and boil down to 8 portions, taken at any time.

    Zi Jin Dan
    For treating prolonged jaundice that does not heal in those with a strong stomach.
    Ingredients:

    • Copper sulfate 2 taels
    • Yellow wax 2 taels
    • 50 large jujubes
      Use a clay pot or silver vessel, add 3 bowls of vinegar, first add the jujubes, simmer for half a day, remove the jujubes, peel and pit them, add the wax next, and simmer 1-2 hours until it becomes a paste. Mix with 2 taels of wax tea and form into pills the size of tung seeds. Each dose is 30 pills, taken with tea or wine. It is also effective for those whose blood is a yellow color and eyes are excessively yellow.[81p]

    　　小茵陈汤韩氏　治发黄，脉沉细，四肢及遍身冷。　　附子一个，炮作八片　炙甘草一两　茵陈二两　　右，用水二升，煮一升，分作三服。
    　　五福饮 【《景岳全书》，下同】 　凡五脏血气亏损者，此能兼治之，足称王道之最。　　人参　熟地黄俱随宜　白朮炒，一钱五分　当归二三钱　炙甘草一钱　　水二锺，煎七分，食远温服。或加生姜三五片。

    　　左归饮　治命门之阴衰阳胜黄疸诸证。　　熟地二三钱或至一二两　山药　枸杞各二钱　炙甘草一钱　茯苓一钱半　山茱萸肉一二钱，畏酸少用。　　水二锺，煎七分，食远服。[82p]

    Xiao Yin Chen Decoction by Han Family: For treating jaundice, with a pulse that is deep and fine, limbs and body feeling cold. One piece of aconite, processed into eight slices; one tael of honey-fried licorice; two taels of Yin Chen. Use two sheng of water, boil down to one sheng, and divide into three doses.

    Wu Fu Drink: For those deficient in the blood and energy of the five organs, this can treat them all, fitting the highest principles of healing. Ginseng and cooked Rehmannia as needed; one and a half qian of fried Atractylodes; two to three qian of Angelica sinensis; one qian of honey-fried licorice. Use two zhongs of water, decoct to seven parts, take warm far from meals. Optionally add three to five slices of fresh ginger.

    Chai Qin Decoction: Treats internal heat combined with external pathogens causing jaundice. Two qian of Bupleurum; two qian of Scutellaria; two qian of Gardenia; two qian of Alisma; two qian of Akebia; one and a half qian of bitter orange. Use two zhongs of water, decoct to eight parts, take warm.

    Chai Ling Decoction: Treats heat in the body accompanied by jaundice, thirst, and diarrhea. Atractylodes, Poria, Alisma, Bupleurum, Polyporus, Scutellaria, combined with water for decoction.

    Zuo Gui Drink: Treats deficiencies in the Yin of the Mingmen with Yang excess and jaundice-related symptoms. Two to three qian of cooked Rehmannia, or up to one to two taels; two qian each of Dioscorea and Goji berries; one qian of honey-fried licorice; one and a half qian of Poria; one to two qian of Chinese cornelian cherry, use less if sour. Use two zhongs of water, decoct to seven parts, take warm far from meals.[82p]

    　　右归饮　治命门之阳衰阴盛黄疸诸证。　　熟地二三钱或加至一二两　山药　枸杞　杜仲姜制，各二钱　山茱萸一钱　肉桂　甘草炙，各一二钱　制附子一二三钱　　水二锺，煎七分，食远温服。

    　　茵陈饮　治前证。
    　　茵陈　栀子　泽泻　青皮各三钱　菊花二钱　甘草一钱　　用水三四锺，煎两锺，不时陆续饮之。
    　　理阴煎　治真阴虚弱黄疸。
    　　熟地三五钱或一二两　当归二三钱或五七钱　炙甘草一二钱　干姜炒黄色，一二三钱　　或加肉桂一二钱　水二锺，煎七八分，热服。
    　　温胃饮　治阴疸。
    　　人参一二三钱或或一两　白朮炒，一二钱或一两　扁豆炒，二钱　陈皮或不用　炙甘草各一钱　干姜炒焦，一二三钱　当归一二钱　　水二锺，煎七分，食远温服。[83p]

    Right Return Decoction treats the symptoms of diminished Yang and excessive Yin at the Mingmen, as well as jaundice. Use 2-3 qian of cooked rehmannia, which can be increased to 1-2 liang; 2 qian each of Chinese yam, goji berries, and eucommia prepared with ginger; 1 qian of cornelian cherry; 1-2 qian each of cinnamon and honey-fried licorice; 1-2-3 qian of prepared aconite. Use 2 zhongs of water, decoct to 7 parts, and consume warm away from meals.

    Major Clear Decoction treats damp-heat jaundice. Use 2 qian each of poria, alisma, and akebia; either double the quantity of gardenia or 1 qian of pigweed, bitter orange, and plantago each; use 1.5 zhongs of water, decoct to 8 parts, and consume warm away from meals.

    Yinchen Decoction treats the previous symptoms. Use 3 qian each of yinchen, gardenia, alisma, and green skin; 2 qian of chrysanthemum; 1 qian of licorice. Use 3-4 zhongs of water, decoct to 2 zhongs, and drink continuously at intervals.

    Regulating Yin Decoction treats deficiency of true Yin leading to jaundice. Use 3-5 qian or 1-2 liang of cooked rehmannia; 2-3 qian or 5-7 qian of angelica; 1-2 qian of honey-fried licorice; 1-2-3 qian of dry ginger, fried until yellow; optionally add 1-2 qian of cinnamon. Use 2 zhongs of water, decoct to 7-8 parts, and consume warm.

    Warm Stomach Decoction treats Yin jaundice. Use 1-2-3 qian or 1 liang of ginseng; 1-2 qian or 1 liang of fried white peony; 2 qian of fried lentils; optionally use dried tangerine peel; 1 qian of honey-fried licorice; 1-2-3 qian of dry ginger, fried until charred; 1-2 qian of angelica. Use 2 zhongs of water, decoct to 7 parts, and consume warm away from meals.[83p]

    　　寿脾煎　一名摄营煎。治脾虚阴黄，中气亏弱等证。　　白朮二三钱　当归　山药各二钱　枣仁钱半　炙甘草一钱　远志制，三五分　干姜炮，一二钱　莲肉炒，二十粒　人参一二钱，急者用一两　　水二锺，煎服。

    疸门

    　　　　单方

    　　食劳黄病，身目俱黄：青矾隔锅煅赤，米酢拌为末，枣肉和丸梧子大。每服二三十丸，食后姜汤下。【《急救方》】
    　　酒疸黄疾，心下懊憹，足胫满，小便黄，饮酒发赤黑黄斑，由大醉当风入水所致。黄蘗三两，木兰一两为末，酒服方寸匕，日三服。【《肘后方》】[84p]

    Shou Pi Jian also known as She Ying Jian. Treats spleen deficiency with yellowing of the skin, weak middle qi, and related symptoms.

    • White Atractylodes (Bai Zhu) 2-3 qian
    • Angelica (Dang Gui) 2 qian
    • Chinese Yam (Shan Yao) 2 qian
    • Jujube Seed (Zao Ren) 0.5 qian
    • Honey-Fried Licorice (Zhi Gan Cao) 1 qian
    • Polygala (Yuan Zhi) 3-5 fen, prepared
    • Dried Ginger (Gan Jiang) 1-2 qian, fried
    • Lotus Seed (Lian Ren) 20 grains, fried
    • Ginseng (Ren Shen) 1-2 qian, use 1 tael for urgent cases
    • Water 2 zhong, decoct and take.

    Wu Jun Zi Jian. Treats spleen and stomach deficiency with cold and dampness accompanying yellowing of the skin.

    • Ginseng (Ren Shen) 2-3 qian
    • White Atractylodes (Bai Zhu) fried in yellow earth 2 qian
    • White Poria (Bai Fu Ling) 2 qian
    • Honey-Fried Licorice (Zhi Gan Cao) 1 qian
    • Dried Ginger (Gan Jiang) fried until yellow 1-2 qian
    • Water 1.5 zhong, decoct and take.

    Comprehensive Collection of Ancient and Modern Medical Writings, Volume 287

    Dian Men

    Single Prescription
    For food-induced yellow sickness, with both body and eyes yellow: calcine blue vitriol in a pot, mix with rice vinegar to make a powder, and combine with jujube meat to form pills the size of a walnut. Take 20-30 pills after meals, followed by ginger broth.
    [From "Emergency Prescriptions"]

    For wine-induced jaundice disease, with discomfort beneath the heart, fullness in the legs and feet, yellow urine, and red-black spots caused by excessive drinking and exposure to wind and water: use 3 qian Huang Lian (Coptis) and 1 qian Magnolia (Mu Lan), ground to powder, take a thumb-sized amount with wine, three times a day.
    [From "Zhou Hou Fang"][84p]

    　　五种黄疸：崔元亮《海上方》云，凡黄有数种，伤酒发黄，误食鼠粪亦作黄。因劳发黄，多痰涕，目有赤脉，益憔悴，或面赤恶心者是也。用秦艽一两銼，作两贴，每贴用酒半斤，浸绞取汁，空腹服。或利便止。就中饮食人易治，屡用得力。
    　　黄病内外皆黄，小便赤，心烦口干：秦艽三两，牛乳一大升，煮取七合，分温再服。《千金方》加芒硝六钱。【《广利方》】
    　　湿热黄疸：柴胡一两，甘草二钱半，作一剂，以水一盏，白茅根一握，煎至七分，任意时时服之。【《秘宝方》】
    　　五种黄病：黄疸、谷疸、酒疸、女疸、劳疸也。黄汗者乃大汗出入水所致，身体微肿，汗出如黄蘗汁。用生茅根一把细切，以猪肉一斤，合作羹食。【《肘后》】
    　　谷疸，因食而得；劳疸，因劳而得。用龙胆一两，苦参三两为末，牛胆汁和丸梧子大，先食以麦饮服五丸，日三服，不止稍增。劳疸加龙胆一两，栀子仁三七枚，以猪胆和丸服之。【《删繁》】[85p]

    Five types of jaundice: Cui Yuanliang in "On Maritime Methods" states that there are several types of jaundice; it can be caused by excessive alcohol consumption or the mistaken ingestion of rat droppings. Yellowing may also occur from overexertion, accompanied by excessive phlegm and snot, red veins in the eyes, increased pallor, or facial redness with nausea. Use one tael of gentian, compounded into two doses, each using half a pound of wine, soaked and squeezed to extract the juice, to be taken on an empty stomach. This method may also yield convenience. Among these, those who are easy to treat with diet often find repeated applications effective.

    Jaundice leads to yellowing both internally and externally, with red urination, and feelings of agitation and dry mouth: use three taels of gentian, one large sheng of cow's milk, boil for seven portions, and take again when warm. The "Thousand Gold Prescriptions" add six qian of mirabilite.

    Damp-heat jaundice: one tael of bupleurum and two and a half qian of licorice, made into one dose, with one cup of water and a handful of white sorgum root, decoct until reduced to seven parts, to be consumed freely at any time.

    The five types of jaundice include: common jaundice, grain jaundice, alcohol jaundice, female jaundice, and labor jaundice. Sweating jaundice occurs due to profuse sweating and entering water, leading to slight body swelling, with sweat resembling yellow berberine juice. Use one handful of fresh sorgum root, finely chopped, with one pound of pork, to prepare a porridge.

    Grain jaundice is acquired through diet; labor jaundice is acquired through exertion. Use one tael of gentian and three taels of bitter cucumber mixed into powder, combined with cow bile to form pills the size of a jujube, and consume five pills prior to meals with wheat drink, three times a day, without stopping until slightly increased. For labor jaundice, add one tael of gentian, three to seven seeds of gardenia, mixed with pig bile to form pills for consumption.[85p]

    　　白黄色枯，舌缩，恍惚语乱者死。当归、白朮二两，水煎入生地汁蜜和服。 【《三十六黄方》】
    　　遍身黄疸：茵陈蒿一把，同生姜一块，捣烂，于胸前四肢，日日擦之。
    　　男子酒疸：用茵陈蒿四根，栀子七个，大田螺一个，连壳捣烂，以百沸白酒一大盏，冲汁饮之，秘方也。
    　　湿热黄疸：灯草根四两，酒水各半，入瓶内，煮半日，露一夜，温服。 【《集元》】
    　　酒疸，黄色遍身者：鹿葱根捣汁服。
    　　黄疸：漆草一杷，捣汁和酒服，不过三五次，即愈。 【《肘后》】
    　　热黄疸疾：萹蓄捣汁，顿服一升。多年者，日再服之。 【《药性论》】
    　　黄疸内热：地丁末，酒服三钱。 【《乾坤秘韫》】
    　　黄疸肿疾：藜芦灰中炮为末，水服五分，小吐。不过数服效。
    　　黄疸喘满，小便自利，不可除热：半夏、生姜各半斤，水七升，煮二升五合，分温再服。有人气结而死，心下暖，以此少许入口，遂活。【仲景】[86p]

    White-yellow withered appearance, retracted tongue, confused speech indicates death. Take two liang of Angelica and Atractylodes, decoct in water, mix with fresh Rehmannia juice and honey, and consume.

    For full-body jaundice: Take a handful of Artemisia capillaris and a piece of ginger, pound them together, and apply to the chest and limbs daily.

    For male alcohol jaundice: Use four stalks of Artemisia capillaris, seven gardenias, and one large river snail, mash them together with shells, and infuse in a large cup of boiling white wine, then drink the juice; it is a secret formula.

    For damp-heat jaundice: Take four liang of light yellow herb root, and half each of wine and water, put it in a bottle, boil for half a day, and let it sit overnight. Consume warm.

    For alcohol jaundice with yellowing all over the body: Mash deer onion root to extract juice and take it.

    For jaundice: One handful of lacquer grass, pound the juice and mix with wine; take no more than three to five times, and you will be cured.

    For heat jaundice disease: Mash cleverweed to extract the juice and take a full liter at once. For chronic cases, consume twice a day.

    For internal heat in jaundice: Take three qian of ground Earthworm and drink with wine.

    For swollen jaundice: Use powdered rush ash, take five fen with water; after a few doses, it will be effective.

    For jaundice with breathlessness, and clear urination, do not remove heat: Take half a jin each of pinellia and ginger, use seven sheng of water, boil down to two and a half sheng, and take in warm doses. There are cases of people dying of qi stagnation; if their heart is warm, taking a little of this can bring them back to life.[86p]

    　　黑黄：面黑黄，身如土色，不妨食，脉沉，若青脉入口者死。宜烙口中黑脉、耳会、玉泉、章门、心俞。用生鬼臼捣汁一小盏服。干者为末，水服。【《三十六黄方》】
    　　酒疸，眼黄脾热：用青(艹舌)蒌焙研，每服一钱，水半盏，煎七分，卧时服，五更泻下黄物立可。名逐黄散。【《普济》】
    　　黑疸危疾：(艹舌)蒌根一片，捣汁六合，顿服，随有黄水从小便出。如不出，再服。
    　　黄疸变黑，医所不能治：用王瓜根汁，平旦温服一小升，午刻黄水当从小便出，不出再服。
    　　五般急黄：山豆根末，水服二钱；若带蛊气，以酒下。
    　　脾劳黄疸：如圣丸。用草血竭、羊膻草、桔梗、苍朮各一两，甘草五钱为末，先以陈酢二杯入锅，用皂矾四两，煎熬良久，下药末，再入白面，不拘多少，和成一块，丸如小豆大，每服三五十丸，空腹酢汤下，一日二服，数日面色复旧也。【《乾坤秘韫》】[87p]

    Black-yellow: The face is black-yellow, the body resembles the color of soil; it is permissible to eat. The pulse is deep; if a blue pulse is felt at the entrance, death follows. It is advisable to cauterize the black pulse in the mouth, the ear meeting point, the Jade Spring, the Chapter Gate, and the Heart Shu point. Use fresh ghost jiao to extract juice and take a small cup. For the dried form, take it as powder with water.

    Alcohol-related jaundice, yellow eyes, and heat in the spleen: Use green (wild) loquat, roast and grind it, taking one qian each time with half a cup of water, decoct until reduced by seven parts, and take it while lying down. In the early hours, it will purge yellow substances immediately. This is called "Expel Yellow Powder."

    Serious black jaundice: One slice of (wild) loquat root, crush to extract juice, take in one breath, and yellow water should pass in urine. If it does not pass, take again.

    If yellow jaundice transforms to black, and the doctor cannot treat it: Use the juice of white melon root, take one small sheng warm in the early morning. By noon, yellow water should be discharged through urine. If not, take again.

    Five types of urgent yellow: Use powdered mountain bean root, take two qian with water; if there is a gu poison, use wine with it.

    Spleen exhaustion jaundice: Like sacred pills. Use one liang each of bloodwort, sheep's sorrel, balloon flower, and fragrant grass, and five qian of licorice as powder. First, use two cups of aged vinegar in a pot, add four liang of alum, boil for a long time, then add the powdered herbs, and mix in white flour, regardless of the amount, until it forms a lump, making pills the size of small beans. Take thirty to fifty pills each time with vinegar soup on an empty stomach, twice a day, and the complexion will return to normal in a few days.[87p]

    　　黄疸如金：薏苡根，煎汤顿服。

    　　黄汗染衣，涕唾皆黄：用蔓菁子捣末，平日以井华水服一匙，日再服，加至两匙以上为度。每夜以帛浸小便，逐日看之，渐白则瘥，不过服五升。
    　　黄疸如金，睛黄，小便赤：用生蔓菁子末，熟水调方寸匕，日三服。 【孙真人食忌】
    　　急黄黄疸，及内黄腹结不通：用蔓菁子捣末，水绞汁服二三钱，当得嚏，鼻中出黄水，及下利则愈。以子压油，每服一盏，更佳。【《拾遗》】
    　　热黄便结：用芜菁子捣末，水和绞汁服，少顷当泻一切恶物，沙石、发草并出。 【《食疗》】
    　　急黄病：苦瓠一枚开孔，以水煮之，绞取汁，滴入鼻中，去黄水。 【《本草》】
    　　黄疸肿满：苦壶卢瓤如大枣许，以童子小便二合，浸一时，取两酸枣大，纳两鼻中，深吸气，待黄水出，良。　　又方：用瓠瓤熬黄为末，每服半钱，日一服，十日愈。然有吐者当详之。 【《伤寒类要》】[88p]

    Jaundice like gold: use coix root, boil into a decoction and take it in one gulp.

    Yellow sweat stains clothes, and both mucus and saliva are yellow: use turnip seeds, grind into powder, and take one spoonful with well water daily, twice a day, increasing to two spoonfuls or more as needed. Each night, soak a cloth in urine, observe it daily, and if it gradually turns white, it indicates recovery; do not take more than five sheng.

    Jaundice like gold, yellow in the eyes, and red urine: use fresh turnip seed powder, mix it with boiled water, and take with a teaspoon three times a day.

    For acute yellow jaundice, and internal yellow abdominal obstruction: use crushed turnip seeds, extract the juice, and take two to three qian; this should induce sneezing, with yellow water coming from the nose, and diarrhea will lead to recovery. Use seeds pressed with oil, taking a cup each time for better effect.

    For hot yellow constipation: use turnip seeds ground into powder, mix with water and extract the juice, shortly this should expel all harmful substances, including sand, stones, and hair.

    For acute yellow disease: take one bitter gourd, pierce it, boil in water, strain to obtain the juice, and drop it into the nose to remove yellow water.

    For swollen jaundice: use bitter gourd pulp about the size of a large jujube, mix with two sheng of a boy's urine, soak for a while, take two sour jujubes and insert them into both nostrils, inhale deeply until yellow water is expelled, which is good. Another method: use gourd pulp, simmer until it turns yellow into powder, take half a qian each time, once daily for ten days until recovery. However, those who vomit should be attended to with care.[88p]

    　　食积黄疸：丝瓜连子烧存性为末，每服二钱。因面得病，面汤下。因酒得病，温酒下。连进数服愈。【《易简》】
    　　黄疸如金：晴明时侵晨，勿令鸡犬妇人见，取东引桃根，细如箸若钗股者一握，细切，以水一大升，煎一小升，空腹顿服。后三五日，其黄离离如薄云散开，百日方平复也。黄散后，可时时饮清酒一杯，则眼中易散，否则散迟。忌食热面猪鱼等物。【《必效》】
    　　急黄喘息，心上坚硬，欲得水吃者：瓜蒂二小合，赤小豆一合，研末，暖浆水五合，服方寸匕，一炊久当吐，不吐再服。吹鼻取水亦可。【《伤寒类要》】
    　　遍身如金：瓜蒂、丁香各四十九枚，砂锅内烧存性为末，每用一字吹鼻，取出黄水；亦可揩牙追涎。
    　　黄疸阴黄：并取瓜蒂、丁香、赤小豆各七枚为末，吹豆许入鼻，少时黄水流出，隔日一用，瘥乃止。【《食疗》】
    　　黄疸初起：柳枝煮浓汁半升，顿服。 【《外台秘要》】[89p]

    Food Accumulation Jaundice: Burn the gourd and seeds together into powder, take two qian each time. If the illness arises from a facial condition, take with soup. If it arises from alcohol consumption, take with warm wine. Repeat several doses to recover.

    Jaundice like Gold: In clear weather during the morning, do not let chickens, dogs, or women see. Take a handful of peach roots, as thin as chopsticks or hairpin. Cut finely, and boil with a large sheng of water until reduced to a small sheng. Take on an empty stomach. After three to five days, the yellowness will disperse like thin clouds, and full recovery will take a hundred days. After the yellow subsides, occasionally drink a cup of clear wine to aid in dispersing; otherwise, the dispersal will be slow. Avoid eating hot noodles, pork, fish, and similar items.

    Acute Yellow with Breathlessness: If there is hardness on the heart and desire for water: take two small gourd stems and one portion of red beans, grind into powder. Mix with five portions of warm water and take a small spoonful. If one does not vomit after a long while, take again. Blowing water through the nose is also acceptable.

    Full-body Gold Color: Take forty-nine gourd stems and forty-nine cloves, burn in a clay pot until reduced to powder. Use a character’s worth to blow into the nose to extract yellow water; can also wipe teeth to stimulate salivation.

    Yin Yellow Jaundice: Take seven each of gourd stems, cloves, and red beans, grind into powder. Blow into the nose a portion the size of a bean; in a short time, yellow water will flow out. Use every other day until healing is achieved.

    Initial Jaundice: Boil half a sheng of willow branches into a concentrated juice and take it all at once.[89p]

    　　五种疸疾：黄疸，谷疸，酒疸，黑疸，女劳疸，黄汗如黄蘗汁，用猪脂一斤，温热服，日三，当利乃愈。【《肘后》】
    　　妇人黄疸，经水不调，房事触犯所致：白矾、黄蜡各半两，陈橘皮三钱为末，化蜡丸梧子大，每服五十丸，以滋血汤或调经汤下。【《济阴》】
    　　血证黄肿：绿矾四两，百草霜一升，炒面半升为末，砂糖和丸梧子大，每服三四十丸，食后姜汤下。【《郑时举传》】　　又方：小麦淘净一斤，皂矾半斤，同炒黄为末，黑枣肉半斤，捣匀，米酢糊为丸梧子大，姜汤下八九十丸，一日三服。【《简便方》】
    　　脾病黄肿：青矾四两，煅成赤珠子，当归四两，酒酻浸七日，焙，百草霜三两为末，以浸药酒打糊，为丸梧子大，每服五丸至七丸，温水下。一月后，黄去立效。此方祖传七世。　　又方：绿矾四两，百草霜、五倍子各一两，木香一钱，为末，酒煎，飞面丸梧子大，每空心酒下五丸。[90p]

    Five types of jaundice: yellow jaundice, valley jaundice, wine jaundice, black jaundice, women's labor jaundice. Yellow sweat like yellow herb juice, take one pound of pig fat, warm and take, three times a day; when it purges, it will cure.

    For women's yellow jaundice, caused by menstrual irregularities and sexual activity: half an ounce each of white alum and yellow wax, three qian of aged orange peel, powdered; form into pills the size of a walnut, take fifty pills with blood-nourishing soup or menstrual regulation soup.

    Blood-related yellow swelling: four ounces of green vitriol, one liter of hundred herbs frost, half liter of fried flour, ground into powder; mix with sand sugar to form pills the size of a walnut, take thirty to forty pills after meals with ginger soup. Another recipe: one pound of cleaned wheat, half a pound of soap alum, fried until yellow and ground into powder; half a pound of jujube flesh, mashed, mixed with rice vinegar to form pills the size of a walnut, take eighty to ninety pills with ginger soup, three times a day.

    For spleen disease yellow swelling: four ounces of green vitriol, calcined into red pearl, four ounces of angelica soaked in wine for seven days, baked; three ounces of hundred herbs frost ground into powder, mix with soaked medicinal wine to form pills the size of a walnut, take five to seven pills with warm water. The yellow will disappear after one month. This recipe has been passed down for seven generations. Another recipe: four ounces of green vitriol, one ounce each of hundred herbs frost and fivefold gall, one qian of wood fragrance, ground into powder, decocted with wine, formed into pills the size of a walnut, take five pills with empty stomach and wine.[90p]

    　　酒黄水肿，黄肿积痛：青矾半斤，酢一大盏，和匀，瓦盆内煅干为度，平胃散、乌药顺气散各半两为末，酢煮糊丸梧子大，每酒或姜汤下二三十丸。不忌口，如锅灰。【《济急方》】
    　　火黄身热，午后却凉，身有赤点或黑黯者，不可治。宜烙手足心、背心、百会、下廉，内服紫草汤。紫草、吴蓝、木香、黄连各一两，水煎服。【《三十六黄方》】
    　　谷疸食劳，头旋心怫郁不安而发黄，由失饥太饱，胃气冲熏所致。苦参三两、龙胆一合为末，牛胆丸梧子大，生大麦苗汁服五丸，日三服。【《肘后方》】
    　　疸黄如金，好眠吐涎：茵陈蒿、白藓皮等分，水二锺煎服，日二服。 【《三十六黄方》】[91p]

    1. For yellow swelling from alcohol, with yellow swelling and accumulated pain: take half a pound of blue vitriol and a large cup of vinegar, mix evenly, and dry in a pottery basin until done. Then take equal parts of Pingwei Powder and Wuyao Shunqi Powder, grind into a fine powder, and form into pills the size of a walnut with the vinegar, taking 20-30 pills with wine or ginger soup. There are no dietary restrictions, like kitchen ash.

    2. For yellow fever with body heat that cools in the afternoon, and the body has red spots or dark blemishes, this should not be treated. It is advisable to cauterize the palms, soles of the feet, the back, the Baihui point, and the lower abdomen, and internally take a Zicao Decoction. Combine one ounce each of purple grass, woad, agarwood, and coptis, and decoct in water for consumption.

    3. For food-related jaundice causing fatigue, with dizziness and difficulty in the heart leading to yellowing of the skin, caused by overeating after hunger, due to qi dysfunction: take three ounces of bitter smartweed and one she (approximately 1/6 ounce) of gentian, grind into powder, form into pills the size of a walnut, and take five pills with fresh barley grass juice, three times daily.

    4. For jaundice that appears golden, causing drowsiness and salivation: combine equal parts of Artemisia capillaris and white skin of lichens, decoct with two sheng (approximately 1.2 liters) of water, and take twice daily.[91p]

    　　伤寒黄疸表热者：麻黄醇酒汤主之。麻黄一把去节，绵裹，美酒五升，煮取半升，顿服取小汗。春月用水煎。【《千金方》】
    　　酒疸，尿黄发黄，心懊痛，足胫满：芫花、椒目等分烧末，水服半钱，日二服。 【《肘后方》】
    　　酒疸脾黄：木鳖子磨酢，服一二盏，见利，效。 【《济急方》】
    　　遍身黄肿：掘新鲜百条根，洗捣罨脐上，以糯米饭半升，拌水酒半合揉软，在药上，以帛包住，待一二日后，口内作酒气，则水从小便中出，肿自消也。百条根，一名野天门冬，一名百奶，状如葱头，其苗叶柔细，一根下有百余个数。【《经验方》】
    　　伤寒发黄：生乌麻油一盏，水半盏，鸡子白一枚，和搅服尽。 【《外台》】
    　　妇人血黄：黄茄子竹刀切，阴干为末，每服二钱，温酒调下。 【《摘元方》】
    　　腹胀黄肿：用亚腰壶卢连子烧存性，每服一个，食前温酒下。不饮酒者，白汤下。十余日见效。【《简便方》】[92p]

    For yellow skin caused by cold-induced fever: The recipe is for a decoction of Ephedra and strong wine. Take a handful of Ephedra without stems, wrap it in cotton, and boil with five sheng of good wine until reduced to half a sheng. Take it in one swift drink to induce slight sweating. In spring, use water for decoction.

    For jaundice from wine, with yellow urine and yellowish complexion, accompanied by heartache and swelling of the feet: Take equal parts of peony flower and pepper, burn them into powder, and consume half a qian with water, twice daily.

    For wine jaundice with spleen yellow: Grind the fruit of the wood vine with vinegar and take one or two cups until improvement is seen.

    For generalized yellow swelling: Dig fresh roots of "Hundred Tails," wash and pound them, then apply on the navel with half a sheng of glutinous rice mixed with half a he of water and wine, kneaded soft. Wrap it in cloth and wait one or two days until a wine scent is produced in the mouth, then water will pass out through urine and the swelling will subside. "Hundred Tails" is also known as wild Asparagus and has a shape similar to a shallot, with soft, fine sprouts containing many small bulbs.

    For yellowing from cold-induced fever: Take one cup of raw sesame oil, half a cup of water, and one egg white, mix well and consume entirely.

    For yellow blood in women: Cut yellow eggplants with a bamboo knife, dry in the shade, grind into powder, and take two qian mixed with warm wine.

    For abdominal swelling and yellowing: Use a Yao stove to cook the seeds of lupin until charred; take one seed before meals with warm wine. For those who do not drink, take with white broth; improvement will be seen in over ten days.[92p]

    　　酒疸：咸平树根白皮捣碎，米酢浸一宿，平旦空腹，温服一二升。 【《开宝》】
    　　食气黄肿，气喘胸满：用不蛀皂角去皮子，酢涂炙焦为末一钱，巴豆七枚，去油膜，以淡酢研好墨，和丸麻子大，每服三丸，食后陈橘皮汤下，日三服。隔一日增一丸，以愈为度。【《经验方》】
    　　时行发黄：竹叶五升切，小麦七升，石膏三两，水一斗半，煮取七升，细服尽剂愈。 【《肘后方》】
    　　房劳黄疸，体重不眠，眼赤如朱，心下块起若瘕，十死一生。宜烙舌下，灸心俞、关元二七壮；以妇人内衣烧灰，酒服二钱。【《三十六黄方》】

    　　酒疸诸疸：用田螺将水养数日，去泥取出，生捣烂，入好酒内，用布帛摅过，将汁饮之，日三服，效。【《寿域》】
